················································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································ The Hope of the Whole 

I sincerely thank you for having a gathering like this today. As I sit quietly and listen to the words, I feel that it is not just one person speaking here, but two people should be speaking. One is the real person, and one is the false person; one is the real person’s words, and one is the false person’s words. 

The title of the message I want to share with you today is "The Hope of the Whole." Let’s talk briefly about "The Hope of the Whole."

Eastern people understand the concept of the whole as heaven (天), earth (地), and humanity (人). 

When we say the whole (全體), what concept do we Eastern people have? We have the concept of heaven, which is heaven (天). Then, what follows? There is the earth, which is earth (地). Then, what follows? There is the concept of humanity (人). In this way, Eastern people have the way of thinking of heaven (天), earth (地), and humanity (人).

So, when we talk about the hope of the whole, it means that there is hope in heaven (天), and then there is hope in the earth (地). It means that there is hope in humanity (人). 

Now, can the hope of heaven, the hope of earth, or the hope of humanity all be different? Or can they be the same? This is an important question.

Using religious terminology, we can say that heaven (天) is God, earth (地) is the earth and all things, and humanity (人) is human beings. If we change this to religious terminology, it comes down to God (神), humanity (人), and things (物). 

There is hope among God, humanity, and all things. So how can we determine that the hope of God, the hope of humanity, and the hope of all things are one hope that cannot be different? This question is a significant issue when we look at history and also when we look at the world stage today.

A good world that God, humanity, and all things desire 

Here, the being called God, the being called heaven, is invisible. Then, who plays the main role? It can be seen that the hope of God is connected through humanity, and the hope of all things is also connected through humanity.

Among humans, what kind of people are there? It is not a problem if there are only good people, but we know that there are also evil people among humans today. 

While there are evil people, religion says that there are evil spirits. Furthermore, there are evil spirits, and alongside evil people, there are also evil substances and evil objects.

So, what do we humans desire? It is to eliminate this evil. It is to remove evil spirits, to remove evil people, and to escape from the position of evil objects. This is the desire of those who are in the evil world, both people and things. As long as evil spirits dominate and have power, we cannot escape. However, when we confirm that there are good spirits, we discover the possibility of turning evil people into good people. 

I believe that by turning evil people into good people, all evil things can also be turned around. 

In the world we live in today, there are families centered on good people.
On one hand, there are evil families, and on the other hand, there are good nations, while there are also evil nations. There is an evil world, but there is also a good world. 

When viewed this way, the world we live in today is not a world centered on good, but rather a fallen world that is under the dominion of evil sovereignty. Therefore, there are obstacles preventing a relationship with God and good spirits in this world. 

In overcoming these obstacles, humanity must play an intermediary role. Thus, the good God has been working through the historical process, centered around the background of religion, to develop a movement to transform the evil world into a good world. 

The world has different ethnic and cultural backgrounds, and different customs and traditions, but it has expanded the scope of religion to form a global religious landscape from a block-level scope. 

Today, there are four major religious cultural spheres: the Christian cultural sphere, the Islamic cultural sphere, the Hindu cultural sphere, and the cultural sphere centered on the Eastern philosophies of Buddhism, Confucianism, and Taoism. Through this religious landscape, efforts are being made to convert people in the evil world into people of the good world. 

If there is a God, then God must have a desire. What is God's desire? It is not for religions to remain as separate entities, but surely to develop one form of religion on a global stage. This must be God's intention. This is something anyone can think about. Not only in thought, but if we were to ask God directly, the answer would be that there must be one religion that represents God's true will in this world. 

God desires one religion, and the countless religious individuals also desire one religion. A religion that can unify the world is the hope and wish of all religious people. Furthermore, all material things in this world should also converge into one realm of goodness through the religious cultural sphere. 

A good world begins with a true individual who is one with God. So, what is the way to bring about the alignment of God's desires, humanity's desires, and the desires of all creation? It must start with a true religious ideal and a true individual who is one with God. 

Does God only desire true individuals? No. What is God's desire? It is to unify religions and, beyond that, to unify the entire world. 

Then, since the world must be unified, and because it has become a fallen world, where evil spirits dominate, God cannot destroy the entire world. Therefore, God must work to expand from one true person on earth. 

When viewed from the perspective of that one true person, God says, "You are the center of the whole hope that represents individuals." Furthermore, if we ask humanity who the standard of true hope is, the answer will be that it is that one person. If we ask all creation who they want to belong to, they will respond that they want to belong to the true person. This one person becomes the subject who can achieve God's individual purpose, humanity's individual purpose, and the individual purpose of all creation. Without this one person, the expansion of families is impossible. 

Then, what desire does humanity have? After individual perfection, humanity desires family perfection. This is a common desire among all humans, and this desire is the same for God. "What kind of family, what kind of ownership do you want?" If we were to ask even a blade of grass or a flower, they would say, "I want to be the flower of a true family owner. I want to be the flower of a family owner rather than an individual owner." 

When we observe this, today, God desires a larger tribe than just a family, and we humans also desire a broader realm of tribal goodness than just a family. All creation desires to become objects of tribal ownership rather than mere family possessions that God loves. When we push forward in this way, God's desire is to make the entire world one. Humanity's desire is also to make the entire world one. All creation wishes to be at the center of a place where God and humanity become one, ruling over all creation as its owner. All creation cannot help but desire this. 

What is a true person? What path can a true person take? This is the question. A true person is someone who possesses the most precious things. What is the most precious thing? It is not having a lot of money. It is not having power. It is not having knowledge. 

Here today, there seem to be many young students, college students. Young students might say, "It's knowledge; I must study." If there are people in business, they might say, "I must earn money." If someone dreams of politics, they might say, "I must gain power." However, we must recognize that these are merely superficial issues. 

No matter how much money one has, that money cannot be passed down to future generations forever. Even if one possesses knowledge, that knowledge cannot be connected to eternity. Even if one has power, it can only be connected to this lifetime. When we ask what is of a higher value that can start from this lifetime and relate to eternity, we find that it is not even one's own life. It is not even one's own life. So what is it? There is nothing but love. There is nothing but love. 

If we were to ask God, "What will you do with this world if you make it one? What do you want from such a world?" God would likely respond, "Ah, it would be good to be one world." Why is it good? What will be done with that goodness? Goodness exists to bring joy, but what will be done with joy? Does God feel sad because He lacks money? Does God feel sad because He lacks knowledge? Does God feel sad because He lacks power? 

There is one thing that God cannot be happy without: love. It is the absence of love that makes Him sad. If God possesses love that can unite God, humanity, and all creation into one, then God becomes a joyful God, a glorious God, and furthermore, a happy God. Therefore, what is the most important thing? The most precious thing is having the power of love that can absorb everything through the heart of God and the heart of humanity. This is the conclusion we arrive at. 

Then, what is the center of the whole? What is the center of the whole desire? The conclusion is true love. When we look at true love, whether one is a true person or not can be evaluated by true truth, but the fundamental issue is that everything is compared and evaluated based on the true love of God. Since the standard of truth is love, the value of truth is determined by the percentage that corresponds to that love. 

Even if one speaks the words of truth, if those words do not align with a loving heart, then even if the words are true, they cannot be considered truly true. Even when speaking true words, one must be a true person who speaks true words after incorporating true love. Only such a person can occupy a central position that all of humanity throughout history desires, or can be considered a person of character. 

Since God cannot find such people in the human world, He substitutes the term "savior" to establish a starting point for the development of a world of love centered around a true person. Thus, the concept of a savior or Messiah is necessary. 

Today in Christianity, Jesus is referred to as Lord, Savior, or Bridegroom, but the issue is not those symbolic terms; the issue is who the central being is. A person who speaks truth while standing in alignment with God's love, a person who acts with true actions motivated by love, a person who lives not according to form and rules but based on God's true love. A person who seeks to save the world not through methods and means but through true love. Such a person is the Messiah, and this is something everyone should understand. 

Then, what is our hope? From such individuals, God desires that a man and a woman come together to form a couple, which is also the hope of humanity and all creation. However, the Messiah may have come to this earth as a son centered on true love, and while he may have become a personal center, he failed to present the tradition of family love centered on messianic love based on a perfected individual personality. 

Today, Christians simply say that Jesus came to die, but that statement seems to be made without much thought or depth. Jesus, as a subject who perfected individual character, was supposed to present the tradition of family love centered on messianic love, but he did not do so in the history of Christianity or before humanity. 

Today, Christians may think, "Whatever the research, it doesn't matter," but that does not hold true. The foundation of a family established on true love has not appeared in the history of humanity. On the foundation of a couple centered on the Messiah, true conjugal love that God can recognize has not been established, nor has the tradition of true parent-child relationships that can love true children. This is the problem. 

If this core had been possible, families would naturally have developed horizontally through historical processes, and a tribal foundation centered on God's love would have been formed. Then, based on the traditions established on the love of each clan, such as the Moon clan, the Kim clan, or the Park clan, a national tradition centered on God's love could have been formed. However, today, on the world stage of historical times, there has not been established a central foundation of tribal and national traditions that can make the true God rejoice and that all humanity and all creation long for. 

Since the tribal foundation has not been established, the national, state, and global foundations have not been established either. Furthermore, there has not yet been established a traditional standard that desires the spiritual and physical worlds to unite centered on God's love. 

Having reached this conclusion, we must reflect and critique our current position. I believe this is a significant resolution that the young men and women gathered here today must consider. 

A young person named Kim, where will you go? It is vague. It is vague. Where will you go? "I will go to Seoul National University, go through graduate school, get a doctorate, and then enter society, achieve success, marry a beloved wife, and have children." But that is trivial! It is trivial. This is no different from an animal. It is trivial. Why do I study? There must be a purpose. 

It exists to expand that stage! How wonderful is that? You and I must become true people, but that truth is not what ordinary people in today's historical times desire. 

As a core that can be the center of the whole desire, standing on the foundation of God's love, as a principled and official law of love that no one can move, we must start as ideal men and women on the path that all people must walk together. That is what heaven desires, what humanity desires, and what all creation desires. The stage where they grow and expand is the central point where the hopes of the entire universe are concentrated. 

Through this couple, who love each other, we can establish a family that connects God's love, and by multiplying children, we can become one like a fortress. Before God, before all humanity, and before all creation, if we can have a family that can be recognized as the center of hope, it would truly be happiness. With that, we can connect to the tribe, connect to national true love, connect to global true love, and connect to the true love of the heavenly kingdom. Without that, everything is in vain. 

When viewed this way, today humanity does not know this content, countless religions do not know this content, and because they do not consider this perspective, Reverend Moon and the followers of Reverend Moon, the members of the Unification Church, and the Unification Church members spread throughout the world are trying to form a new personal base, family base, tribal base, national base, and global base in front of this world. 

That is a developmental stage on a straight line, but there is only one path. What is it? It is the path that can connect to true love, and it can only be possible by laying down the bridge to that love. Therefore, the members of the Unification Church must present this movement. I believe this is an important issue that everyone gathered here today must awaken to and recognize. (Applause) 

True religion is a sacrificial religion. 

However, while trying to walk this path of love, this world is devoid of such love and is entirely evil. Therefore, naturally, one will encounter the path of suffering, and this is how it is viewed. For this reason, all true religions that follow God must walk the path of suffering. 

How do we distinguish between a good person and an evil person among two people? The person who is willing to put in less effort is closer to the evil side. The person who is willing to put in more effort in public matters leans toward the good side. This is something you should recognize, as it occurs dozens of times a day, or even hundreds of times in severe cases, in our daily lives. 

Then, how do we measure what is good and what is evil? In the realm of ethics and morality, the concept of good and evil is measured by whether one suffers less or willingly suffers more. To willingly suffer more means to walk the path of suffering accompanied by the bond of love. 

What does that mean? It means that in absorbing and digesting the foundation of the private evil world, one does not suppress it with a public heart of love but rather overcomes difficulties through patience. A person who stands in such a position is a good person, generally speaking. 

What does religion do? Of course, religious people must also put in effort. Taking it to a higher level, true religion is not a religion that merely works hard; it is a religion that sacrifices. It is a religion that incorporates one's own desires.
is not the case, but rather a religion that sacrifices for true love in place of the public will of God is what belongs to true religion.  
Today, countless religious people around the world are faced with the mission of fulfilling God's true love globally, yet they fail to take responsibility to tackle the evil world with greater sacrifice and love, instead acting for the benefit of their own denominations, their relatives, and individual believers. I recognize this as an unforgivable sin.  
For this reason, the Unification Church must sacrifice individuals to save families, sacrifice families to save tribes, sacrifice tribes to save nations, sacrifice nations to save the world. Such a thought has never existed in history.  
When I say this, those who are here for the first time today might say, "Moon is teaching to sacrifice the nation, so what..." but that is a misunderstanding. When the day comes to sacrifice the nation centered on such love, the center of the nation will not be south of the 38th parallel, but will be determined at the center of many nations.  
I want to dwell in love, I want to rest in love, I want to give and receive through love, I want to sing through love, and I want to cry out for happiness through love. This is the principle. That love is not human love but public true love. If a nation and people can become such, then that nation and people will have the ability to move the world, move the heavenly kingdom, and even move God.  
Today, our Unification Church has faced persecution before this nation and people, has faced persecution in Asia, and has faced persecution before the nations of the world. But what is the reason that those here have not perished and have survived in such a gap? There is a power to break through the cracks. Just as water leaks out of a hole, there is such power. There is a power that cannot be blocked by human power, any knowledge, or any wealth. What is that? It is the power motivated by true love. That is what exists.  
Do not live centered on the individual.  
From that perspective, today, the Republic of Korea is shouting for a human revolution and advocating for a subjectivity ideology, but if that human revolution is only for the Republic of Korea, who will carry out the human revolution for the world? Who will carry out the human revolution for the universe? If we do not connect to a dimension that transcends the Republic of Korea, it will become isolated.  
When we think of this, thinking of a consistent path of liberation and a consistent path of victory is to think of a nation of a higher dimension, and having such thoughts while being patriotic is the way to practice high-level patriotism. When we enter families with such thoughts, we become true families of a higher dimension. When we hold such thoughts and show filial piety before our parents, we become true filial sons and daughters of a higher dimension.  
You have now come to understand the principles. You are aware of the struggles within your body and mind. The struggle within the individual leads to struggles within families, and when families struggle, tribes struggle, and this gradually expands into wars.  
Therefore, in this externally developed world, there is no way to find an ideal standard. Theoretically, it does not match. Where do we cultivate the unified foundation of our body and mind that originated from my individual being? No matter how strong a person’s mind is, no matter how much I try to dominate my body and do as I please, I discover that I am being dragged along. However, if the mind can completely occupy the body and can unify completely, if I establish my body with a heart of true love, even if the body tries to escape or resists, it will not resist. The more it moves, the faster the human heart will turn.  
If humans had not fallen, the mind and body of humanity centered on God's love would not have been able to stand in an absolutely contradictory position, but because of the fall, they found themselves in such a position. Therefore, to reestablish the historical path and prepare a base to settle a world of peace, the providence of salvation, or in the case of the Unification Church, the providence of restoration, is a tedious religious consciousness, and through religious rites, we weave the history of suffering, sacrifice, and bloodshed. You must understand this fact.  
From this perspective, the problem is simple. The problem is simple. If we create men and women centered on true love from God, families will automatically be formed, and as this number increases, it is a good wish that anyone desires, so it will develop rapidly over time. Thus, the formation of nations, states, and the world becomes possible. This is what heaven desires. You must know this and understand where you are positioned today.  
If you are centered on the individual and have such desires, those desires are good. They are not to be discarded. Earn money, but do so based on God's love. Spend money not just for your own feelings or for yourself, but for your nation and the world, based on God's love.  
Learning is also good. Knowledge is good. Learn. However, if you study to achieve success and build your living foundation, that is trivial. Through learning, to quickly save the ignorant world and connect it to the world of love centered on the overall desire, it is principled that a knowledgeable person leads rather than an ignorant one. Therefore, I pursue this path, and how wonderful it is to say that I will go this way to save the majority of humanity in a short time.  
Do not engage in schemes and slanders to become a leader, and do not forcefully bring down those who do not qualify. If you engage in sacrificial service, you must automatically be pushed forward and become someone who possesses power.  
This is a path that is different from what human history has drawn and what we see in the living environment today. It is a path of a higher dimension among religious paths, and if God exists, He will surely come through this path... God does not come through families immediately. God's first desire is the nation. It is one world. He comes to find a nation through the world, finds a people through the nation, finds a tribe through the people, finds a family through the tribe, and finds the individual through the family. Yet, people jump and throw everything away, saying, "God, just come to me and love me." A religion with such a thieving mindset will perish. (Applause)  
Nothing can dominate true love.  
Today, even though it is not hot, I feel like I am getting too heated. Do you understand what I am saying? "Yes." I have to say a lot... I could not sleep for two hours. I am sorry for being a bit late as I hurried here, but I do not feel guilty. It is a bit of an inconvenience to be late in front of you, but I do not feel guilty because this gathering is more precious than any gathering of the Unification Church, so even if I am late... I see this gathering as less important than this Holy Youth Association gathering, so I do not feel guilty. (Laughter, applause) But why do you all react like this? You should say, "Teacher, it is late," but why are you applauding? What does that mean? It means, "The way of heaven follows him." It means, "Even though you are late, you did well, teacher." (Applause) Now, you understand the content.  
Then, Reverend Moon, why are you being scorned and struggling? It is to test what true love is and whether you have united with God's love! How harsh is that test? When you pass through that harshness, the conclusion is that you are a truly harsh person. A truly harsh person, that is a dream.  
So, I hit the families of the Unification Church. Hit, hit, hit, die, die, die, but it seemed like they would die, yet they did not die, and it seemed like they would perish, yet they survived. How? Because of love. There is nothing that can dominate love. There is nothing that can dominate true love. How wonderful is that!  
Those who do not know this will see the Unification Church as nothing. When they see it, it may seem shabby, but if it moves, it looks like a day goblin in the daytime and a night goblin at night. It seems strange. However, there is nothing strange about it. We are sparked by the string of love, the electric wire of love. Spark. Regarding believing in the Unification Church, parents are saying, "Reverend Moon, you are a love thief who took our sons and daughters." Did I take them? They threw them away themselves. They do not give love, and when they come here and taste the sweet flavor of love, they follow. It is nothing special.  
Students, now that you understand, do not boast about attending Seoul National University from now on. I do not see it as something great. How many hours do you study in a year? Even if you think you study seven hours a day, if you catch five days a week, that is 35 hours (5×7=35). If you catch 100 days, how much is that? 700 hours. Then, if you catch 300 days, how much is that? About 2000 hours. If you divide that by 24 hours, how much is that? It amounts to only a few days. Do not boast about that and act presumptuously.  
What is better than that is love. There is no love more precious than that, which cannot be learned in an instant. The practical power of love moves based on eternity. It requires a long time. One year. You cannot pass in two years. Even after 10, 20, 30, or 40 years, you cannot obtain a diploma. The dimension keeps rising, and it comes back to touch you.  
You can obtain a doctoral degree in any field of study, but the process of the philosophy of love is infinite, infinite. Yet, that does not make you bored or exhausted. It is simply enjoyable, happier than anything in the world, and you feel grateful and dignified.  
Be the center of love, the hope of the whole, as a young person.  
Now, why do I say this? Young people, especially where will the Republic of Korea go now? We must not spare effort and sacrifice to digest North Korea. Based on the digestion of the North and South, we must digest the democratic world and the communist world. With what? With money? With power? That will not work. The United States started with power, but it has all ended. The Soviet Communist Party started with power, but it has all ended. With what? With true love.  
Jesus spoke of love when he said, "Pray for your enemies," but that love can no longer be found in Christianity. Unless a new era comes to blow a storm into the dry church lacking love and plant the seeds of love, all religions will perish. Our Unification Church is also one of those religions, so it cannot perish, but must be the seed of love...  
My eyes, my gaze, are fired through the word love. My hearing listens through the sound waves of love. My strength arises through the power of love. It may seem like it will perish, but it will prosper. After working hard and sacrificing, what happens? Because it is centered on love, it is destined to reach the center. If you do not stop for the nation and continue such sacrifices, when you make a full turn, it is a fortune that keeps turning, so if you keep turning, you will inevitably reach the center.  
Today, young people do not know this. Those who sacrifice will inevitably become the center. In families, the filial son is the one who sacrifices more. Therefore, he becomes the center of the family. The patriot of the nation is the one who sacrifices more, so he becomes the center of the nation. Among saints, the one who sacrifices more becomes the center among saints. This is the way of heaven, and we must solemnly follow this path and create people who can harmonize in all fields, which is called "Seonghwa" (成和). Do you understand what Seonghwa youth is? It is a youth who can harmonize with heaven, humanity, and all things. Where such youth go, new hopes sprout. It is where God's new hope dwells, and the power of God's love increases. Knowing this amazing fact, I hope you will embrace this infinite love...  
Today, Reverend Moon, who has faced persecution and opposition, has laid the foundation to bridge the gap among all races and present issues to the world. You are the same. You are the same. When you extend this thought into society, the Republic of Korea will become a glorious nation. Knowing that the world hopes for this, I hope you will renew your resolve and determination, and I hope you will become the center of love for the whole. Can you do that? "Yes." (Applause)  
As long as the Unification Church walks this path, it will break through the cracks of persecution and sprout. Knowing that this is undeniable truth, I hope many young people will emerge, and on this commemorative day, I hope you will understand what I have said. Amen! "Amen!" (Applause)  
[Prayer] Beloved Father! We recall once again that the day of victory is desired by all humanity, by true humanity, by all creation, by the entire universe, and even by heaven.  
What is miserable due to lack? It is not miserable due to lack of money, nor lack of power and authority, nor lack of knowledge. When we look at the desolate wilderness of this end-time world without true love, there is no way to block the misery of that view, and when we hear the cries of humanity starving for love, we feel the pain of our hearing being shattered. Father, please look down upon this end-time era we face.  
Even if this world is destined to perish, we have the responsibility to awaken it with the whip of love. You, who know this, have planted the seeds of Your love in a corner of this earth, in a place like a dung heap, and until it sprouts and takes root in the ground, it was treated as a flower of dung, a smelly heap, but when it takes root in the ground, that dung heap becomes fertilizer, leaving a foundation of happiness for a thousand years and establishing an unbreakable foundation of love, tracing the amazing heart of the Father.  
The wish of the Unification Church members connected through this one child standing here, their dream, and the destination of their happiness is to achieve true love that can connect with You. They are a group yearning for such true love, a sorrowful group, a group of reconciliation, and You know this well.  
Now, over 60 years old, every time I come to this nation and people, I see the confrontation between the North and South, and I recall the old days when I prayed before You while crossing the 38th parallel, feeling anxious and hurried, but no one knows this.  
I have not forgotten for a moment the times I prayed and wept while standing with one foot on the 38th parallel, vowing to drive out Kim Il-sung and the North Korean Communist Party. Until this day, I have fought and bled on the front lines of victory. At such times, whenever I discover that heaven is working in an even lonelier place, in the place of friends, I have come to know heaven's gratitude. Even if I stand in a sorrowful position of being chased by my people, I am comforted by the thought that the day will come when love's flowers will bloom.
Even if it means my blood boiling and my bones drying up, I cannot forget these past days that are unforgettable. Now, considering the urgent steps that this nation must take in the midst of the significant global situation over the next three years, I realize that it is not only the wish of the Republic of Korea but also the wish of the heavenly kingdom and the desire of humanity in the free world to turn each and every one of the 38 million people into victors who can digest communism, regardless of misunderstandings or persecution, facing both North and South.

Knowing such things, I ask you, Father, to protect and remember these members of the Unification Church who are silently moving like ants carrying food home, even if the sun sets. We believe that we cannot perish before heaven abandons us. May you be their strength and the wall of love, so that even if they are showered with all the arrows of evil, they may have the faith that all will break upon this wall of love. I hope that the days of blessing will not depart from them. Please do not let your hand of love depart from all the members of the Unification Church.

Now, even as I hear news that some are collapsing in prisons and some are falling at execution sites in the underground of Eastern European communist satellite states, I am responsible for this path that must be commanded. (Praying while crying) Father, who knows the stark misery and the internal situation of the Unification Church, please look down upon us.

Even if tomorrow's master disappears without a shadow, my wish is to bloom as a flower upon your name and the grave of your love. Beyond that, I have no other desires. I have sacrificed all that I have, my blood and my possessions, so that this nation can become a country that can boast to the world... This poor 5,000-year history, a whirlpool of misery that cannot boast anything before the world, embracing this sorrowful history of lamentation, I have come to understand that it is your will for it to become a foundation where the flag of pride and victory can be planted. Since I have come to know that you want me to drive iron pillars into this whirlpool to build this foundation, I have quietly come forth, and now it is becoming evident on the surface of the water, and the time when this can be revealed in the mountains is gradually approaching. I thank you once again for this, which is due to your utmost sincerity and the protection of your love.

Please recreate the explosive point of love in the hearts of the young people gathered here. May they become the young people who cannot go without moving, who cannot rest without shouting, and may they become the leaders of tomorrow's nation and a lighthouse of the world, guiding all ships of humanity toward the heavenly kingdom across the dark sea of death. I earnestly wish for this, Father. I truly hope and desire it.

I thank you for this gathering today, and I hope that you will increase your protection and whip before the path of the Unification Church that is hastening its steps from the 3,000-ri coast to the world. I earnestly request and wish that they may become heavenly warriors and soldiers who, taking the path of sacrifice as hope, draw the traditional history of tomorrow's victory, with a steadfast and strong gaze directed toward the enemy.

I hope that the grace and love of all things will be abundant in their future, and I ask once again that you pour out the gift of life upon the groups of unification working around the world at this time, and grant the power of resurrection to the world of the words conveyed. I pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.*
